298_CD 37_CD Financial_NNP instruments_NNS a_DT Derivatives_NNS Derivatives_NNS are_VBP financial_JJ instruments_NNS that_WDT derive_VBP their_PRP$ value_NN from_IN the_DT price_NN of_IN an_DT underlying_JJ item_NN such_JJ as_IN equities_NNS ,_, bonds_NNS ,_, interest_NN rates_NNS ,_, foreign_JJ exchange_NN ,_, credit_NN spreads_NNS ,_, commodities_NNS or_CC equity_NN and_CC other_JJ indices_NNS ._.
i_FW Types_NNPS of_IN derivatives_NNS Derivative_JJ instruments_NNS are_VBP classified_VBN as_IN being_VBG for_IN either_DT trading_NN or_CC hedging_VBG purposes_NNS ._.
The_DT following_VBG outlines_VBZ the_DT nature_NN and_CC terms_NNS of_IN the_DT most_RBS common_JJ types_NNS of_IN derivatives_NNS used_VBN by_IN HSBC_NNP ._.
Currency_NNP forwards_RB represent_VBP commitments_NNS to_TO purchase_VB foreign_JJ or_CC domestic_JJ currency_NN at_IN a_DT future_JJ date_NN ._.
Forward_RB rate_NN agreements_NNS are_VBP individually_RB negotiated_VBN interest_NN rate_NN futures_NNS that_WDT call_VBP for_IN a_DT cash_NN settlement_NN at_IN a_DT future_JJ date_NN for_IN the_DT difference_NN between_IN a_DT contractual_JJ rate_NN or_CC agreed_VBD rate_NN of_IN interest_NN ,_, and_CC the_DT current_JJ market_NN rate_NN ,_, based_VBN on_IN a_DT notional_JJ principal_NN amount_NN ._.
Currency_NNP and_CC interest_NN rate_NN swaps_NNS are_VBP commitments_NNS to_TO exchange_VB one_CD set_NN of_IN cash_NN flows_NNS for_IN another_DT ._.
Swaps_NNS result_VBP in_IN an_DT economic_JJ exchange_NN of_IN currencies_NNS or_CC interest_NN rates_NNS for_IN example_NN ,_, fixed_VBN rate_NN for_IN floating_VBG rate_NN or_CC a_DT combination_NN of_IN both_DT of_IN these_DT i._FW e._FW cross-currency_NN interest_NN rate_NN swaps_NNS ._.
Except_IN for_IN certain_JJ currency_NN swaps_NNS ,_, no_DT exchange_NN of_IN principal_JJ takes_VBZ place_NN ._.
Equity_NN swaps_NNS are_VBP bilateral_JJ agreements_NNS to_TO transfer_VB the_DT risk_NN and_CC returns_NNS on_IN an_DT equity_NN in_IN exchange_NN for_IN a_DT stream_NN of_IN payments_NNS ,_, typically_RB interest_NN ._.
Foreign_JJ currency_NN ,_, equity_NN and_CC interest_NN rate_NN options_NNS are_VBP contractual_JJ agreements_NNS under_IN which_WDT the_DT seller_NN writer_NN grants_NNS the_DT purchaser_NN holder_NN the_DT right_NN ,_, but_CC not_RB the_DT obligation_NN ,_, either_CC to_TO buy_VB a_DT call_NN option_NN or_CC sell_VB a_DT put_NN option_NN at_IN or_CC by_IN a_DT set_NN date_NN or_CC during_IN a_DT set_NN period_NN ,_, a_DT specific_JJ amount_NN of_IN a_DT foreign_JJ currency_NN or_CC a_DT financial_JJ instrument_NN at_IN a_DT predetermined_VBN price_NN ._.
In_IN consideration_NN for_IN the_DT assumption_NN of_IN foreign_JJ exchange_NN ,_, equity_NN ,_, or_CC interest_NN rate_NN risk_NN ,_, the_DT seller_NN receives_VBZ a_DT premium_NN from_IN the_DT purchaser_NN ._.
Options_NNS may_MD be_VB either_RB exchange-traded_JJ or_CC negotiated_VBN between_IN the_DT Group_NNP and_CC a_DT customer_NN on_IN an_DT over_IN the_DT counter_JJ basis_NN ._.
Futures_NNS are_VBP exchange-traded_JJ agreements_NNS to_TO buy_VB or_CC sell_VB a_DT standard_JJ quantity_NN of_IN a_DT specified_VBN fixed_JJ income_NN security_NN ,_, time_NN deposit_NN ,_, equity_NN or_CC currency_NN at_IN a_DT future_JJ date_NN ,_, at_IN a_DT price_NN decided_VBD at_IN the_DT time_NN the_DT contract_NN is_VBZ made_VBN ._.
Equity_NN futures_NNS may_MD be_VB settled_VBN in_IN cash_NN or_CC through_IN delivery_NN ._.
Credit_NNP default_NN swaps_NNS are_VBP bilateral_JJ agreements_NNS to_TO transfer_VB credit_NN risks_NNS between_IN counterparties_NNS ._.
Under_IN the_DT agreement_NN ,_, the_DT party_NN buying_VBG protection_NN makes_VBZ one_CD or_CC more_JJR payments_NNS to_TO the_DT party_NN selling_VBG protection_NN during_IN the_DT life_NN of_IN the_DT swap_NN in_IN exchange_NN for_IN an_DT undertaking_NN by_IN the_DT seller_NN to_TO make_VB a_DT payment_NN to_TO the_DT buyer_NN following_VBG a_DT specified_VBN credit_NN event_NN ._.
Credit_NNP default_NN swaps_NNS may_MD be_VB on_IN a_DT single_JJ name_NN counterparty_NN or_CC may_MD be_VB on_IN multiple_JJ names_NNS counterparties_NNS ._.
Commodity_NNP derivatives_NNS include_VBP exchange_NN traded_VBN and_CC over_IN the_DT counter_NN contracts_NNS involving_VBG commodities_NNS and_CC base_NN metals_NNS ._.
ii_FW Use_NN of_IN derivatives_NNS Commercially_RB HSBC_NNP transacts_NNS in_IN derivatives_NNS for_IN three_CD primary_JJ purposes_NNS to_TO create_VB risk_NN management_NN solutions_NNS for_IN clients_NNS ,_, for_IN proprietary_JJ trading_NN purposes_NNS ,_, and_CC to_TO manage_VB and_CC hedge_VB HSBCs_NNP own_JJ risks_NNS ._.
For_IN accounting_VBG purposes_NNS ,_, derivative_JJ instruments_NNS are_VBP classified_VBN as_IN either_DT trading_NN or_CC hedging_NN ._.
Trading_NN Derivatives_NNS Most_JJS of_IN the_DT Groups_NNS derivative_JJ transactions_NNS relate_VBP to_TO sales_NNS and_CC trading_NN activities_NNS ._.

Trading_NN derivatives_NNS are_VBP valued_VBN at_IN mark-to-market_NN based_VBN on_IN quoted_VBN market_NN prices_NNS or_CC on_IN internally_RB developed_VBN models_NNS that_WDT are_VBP based_VBN on_IN independently_RB sourced_JJ market_NN parameters_NNS ,_, including_VBG interest_NN rate_NN yield_NN curves_NNS ,_, option_NN volatilities_NNS and_CC currency_NN rates_NNS ._.
